<Review>I posted during the process, but now that it's completed I've included before and after photos. We started off thinking we wanted a paver area for a fire pit and then the ideas evolved from there. We received quotes from nearly a dozen companies to do pavers and/or turf and ultimately decided on System Pavers after all the great help and insight from Albert the designer. He was great helping us come up with a vision for the backyard and the pricing was competitive. <review>Really surprised by all the excellent reviews. That is how I chose them too. I got 'Brandon' as my tech and 'Nick' as the sales associate. Their prices were 20% more than other quotes but given I really wanted a quality work I did not mind. They have nice vans and logo but that is where it ended for me. Here is the chronology of facts. I had two shower glass custom install in Los Altos, a Neo-Angle shower and a Regular shower.

Visit 1 : Brandon does Measurements. He is very happy with quality of shower framing and tile-work and says everything is plumb and within 1/8th tolerance.

Visit 2 : Install appointment. Neo-angle shower door ordered '2 inches' short! Hardware Finishes ordered wrong. Other shower get installed but they don't have the poly door stops.

Visit 3: They bring the correct hardware. Both showers get installed and after hours of messing around with installation Brandon claims everything is in order. However there is a gap between pony wall and shower door that he can not fit any kind of poly stops. If you spray the hand-shower toward that area water will just leak out but since this is a master shower and not gonna be used by kids I move on.

I test the showers next day and

A) they grossly leak from under the panes and around the bottom hinges. Upon examination he did not silicon around any hinges and the bottom silicon bead is not fully filling the bottom gap between glass pane and the curb.

B) the door on the regular shower rubs against the door stop.

Visit 4:  Brandon refills the silicon and readjust the doors

Next day I test the showers and still one hinge leaking. At this point I give up on these guys and figure out the "excellent customer service" means we are willing to stop by as many times as you want till you give up ! I take the matter in my own hands and redo the silicon around all hinges and the hinge leak issue is now fixed. Few months into the shower there is still numerous problems:

A) I figured one of my glass panes is actually warped !!  First time in my life I see warped glass. This makes only the top and bottom corner of the door hit the poly stop and after couple of months the poly stop split in half at the top and bottom due to the warped door hitting the stop at only two strike points, instead of sitting flush against the full length.

B) multiple alignment issues. Tolerances not met. Door will run against poly stops  as shower gets hot. The panes misalign in all dimensions.

I have just lived with the imperfections and did not bother calling these folks again for yet another lame visit. Guess will just burn another 6-7K and have someone competent come redo the whole thing from scratch.

If you are looking for a precision job, run away. Or maybe I just got unlucky with my Tech and their others techs are better.<//review><pics>None</pics>< response>

< user_name>
Sam Mercado</user_name>
<time>1551559468612</time><Rate>5< /Rate>< text>
A small, tidy, no-nonsense place for breakfast and lunch that the locals obviously frequent. We were there early on a bright Saturday morning where a least half the customers greeted Carla like regulars.
The place is located in a nondescript, semi-rural area on the south edge of Greenfield. It's almost like a holdover from Mayberry RFD, except for the flat screen TV on one side of the back wall. One fellow at the counter having coffee and reading the paper was wearing bib overalls, while a couple of farmers next to him chatted about the previous night's rain. Breakfast portions were generous, satisfying, and moderately priced. Carla's service is prompt, efficient, and amicable.</text>

< Review>
My dog (Claire) has had an enlarged heart now for a couple years. She has been on numerous medications and there finally came a time where the lasik just quit working. She was filling up with fluids in her belly and I was having my vet drain her with a needle and syringe. My vet had to have her heavily sedated as she would fight them putting the needle in her (one time the needle actually ripped her skin). As she continued to fill with the fluids, I was out of town visiting my folks and decided to go see Dr Scheidt as she was my vet in Fresno before I moved to the Bay Area. Not only did she and her amazing staff not have to sedate her, they removed more fluids than the previous vet without having to sedate her. They said their approach was a bit different than other vets. What I found after having this done several times with Sierra View Animal Hospital is that Dr Scheidt and her staff, have a care for their animals that I have never experience before. They are in this for the right reasons, to give your pet the best quality care they possibly can. Unfortunately the time came on Friday when I had to put my precious Claire down. Dr Scheidt and her staff helped me make the right decision based on Claire's condition. I cannot say enough about the quality of service that I received from Sierra View Animal Hospital. Although I live in the Bay Area, I will make the drive to Fresno to have my next pet receive the best quality of service that SVAH provides. Thank you again Dr Scheidt and your staff for taking such great care of my baby girl.<//Review>

<name>Michael Longley</name><Pics>None<//Pics><Review>I brought my daughter here to get her tongue pierced. She was considering getting two piercings side by side and called a few piercing studios to discuss this beforehand. The advice she got on the phone from here was the most comprehensive and in depth and we got the impression that their main concern was her health and happiness with the piercing she was getting rather than what would make them the most money so we chose to come here.

Upon arrival we were greeted by Danny who it turns out was the same guy she had spoken to on the phone. She opted to just get the single tongue piercing in the end but Danny still took the time to explain exactly what was different about doing the two different piercings and what the possible things which could go wrong were.

He already mentioned on the phone that if you get two side by side then because of the anatomy of the tongue there is a slight possibility you can damage the nerves in the tongue and lose sensation or taste on part of your tongue, although this is very rare. We really appreciated his up front honesty about this, however small the risk it is something you need to know before you make your decision and it was something that NONE of the other studios we called had even mentioned.

Everything was sterilised while he explained exactly what he was going to do, and his knowledgeable and friendly manner really helped set my daughter at ease.

She opted to have the piercing positioned a little further back than most people have it and once it was done I was concerned that when her tongue swells up there might not be enough free room on the bar to allow for the swelling, as the tongue is a bit thicker there. Without a moments hesitation and with no prompting from us Danny immediately offered to swap the bar out for a slightly longer one to put our minds at ease.

All told I was extremely happy with the friendly and professional attitude Danny exhibited throughout our whole dealings with the store. We have had piercings done in several studios around the world and this was easily the best experience we have ever had. I would recommend Danny to anyone.</Review>< response>

I am a Holistic Health Practitioner of 10 years and the Sacramento Chapter Leader of the Weston A Price Foundation for 5 years running an over 1,000 member online community of healing practitioners, farmers, parents and other community members discussing nutrition all day long in seriously complex conversations.  I was so excited to discover the Backbone Cafe because they have some incredibly important practices of cooking that promote health woven into their menu.  First off they have bone broth by the mug, which is an incredibly powerful gut, bone and joint remedy, and they prepare it properly with pasture raised, local meat.  They serve naturally gluten free meals for people with Celiac, and their bread comes from Grateful Bread which I believe takes the time to actually ferment their grains with wild yeast, which breaks down the Phytic Acid which makes it much easier to digest.
Also they utilize the animal fat from the pasture raised animals, and have NO Canola Oil, Soy, or other problematic oils, using only animal fat, coconut oil and avocado oil, or Ghee, which makes me so excited.  As a huge advocate for the traditional fats such as lovingly raised animal fat, butter, coconut oil, olive oil, palm oil, avocados and more, I was so happy to see they had gotten the most important thing right for good health, quality fat.  Considering our own natural food co-op is still utilizing Canola Oil in spite of all the research about how unhealthy it is because of cost I am guessing, and I will not eat so many of their house prepared food because of that reason, I was so grateful that Backbone Cafe is not using it at all.

I love their menu, I love the food and drinks we got here, and the only things I wish they would add in the future is fermented vegetables to their meals, or in my dream world raw milk and house made fermented fruit and tea drinks, however California's regulations around restaurants and food for sale would have to be changed for that to be even a possibility, but hey maybe if I add it to my Google review then one day California Lawmakers will stop making it so hard for traditionally prepared foods and drinks to be sold to community so that we can restore our health naturally and affordably.< /Text>

<Rating>3</Rating>< Review>
Very friendly staff, I love the concept! I'm always looking for organic as well as low carb for dietary needs and it confuses me that this combo is very hard to find even in what should be 'healthy' cafes. The food was delicious! Prices are what you'd expect when choosing contrary to the mainstream eaters, but being that I have to ask them to hold ingredients I personally can't eat, I get very little food for the price. This is a lovely place though for you all, don't hesitate if you're looking for 'outside the box nutrition'. Charging me full price when I take the dish down to half it's size is the norm at all locations so I don't fault them, I only wish a place like this could be more understanding and value my decision to still come and reward me with a lower cost. But until a perfect world, I would not judge this great place.< /Review>

<Review>I frequently wonder how Stater Bros. can justify the prices for their produce. It always looks like it's gone 10 rounds with Mike Tyson and had to be put in a medically induced coma to recover. Their prices on most non-food items are on par with most grocery stores, which is about + $1-3 more than you would pay at Target or Walmart. Their selection is limited for most food items, which means a few big name brands and then their own brand. If you just need basic items, Stater Bros. will have something- it might not be the quality you're used to, but it will probably have the item. Their meat selection is very limited compared to other grocery stores. If you're shopping for meat, shop elsewhere. Same with bakery and deli items, most Stater Bros. don't have a dedicated counter for them to be ordered from, just a cold case or a few shelves.

So, if you have an option, go to a different grocery store. If you don't, you'll probably find some form of what you're looking for at Stater Bros.</Review>< time>
